Can be countered with Cure potions.\\n- **Devastating Bite**: The boss bites opponents, dealing damage, healing itself, and gaining resistance for 100 ticks.\\n- **Custom Summoning**: Summon the boss using a custom recipe crafted with bones, wither skeleton heads, and a wither star.\\n\\n## Installation\\n\\n1. Build the mod: `./gradlew build`\\n2. Place the JAR file in your mods folder\\n3. Launch Minecraft with Forge 1.20.1\\n\\n## Usage\\n\\n### Summoning the Boss\\nCraft a summoning item using:\\n- 4x Bones\\n- 3x Wither Skeleton Heads\\n- 1x Wither Star (center)\\n\\nPlace this item on the ground to summon the Undead Dragon Boss.\\n\\n## Boss Mechanics\\n\\n### Miasma\\n- Boss releases miasma clouds at regular intervals\\n- Miasma poisons and damages nearby players\\n- Apply Cure potions to negate miasma damage\\n\\n### Bite Attack\\n- Boss lunges at nearby players\\n- Deals significant damage\\n- Heals the boss for 25% of damage dealt\\n- Grants the boss Resistance effect for 100 ticks\\n\\n## Development\\n\\nThis mod is built with Minecraft Forge 1.20.1 and uses Java 17.\\n\\n## License\\n\\nMIT License\\n\"}]}",

massive undead dragon boss with unique mechanics and powerful weapon drops.\\n\\n## Features\\n\\n### Boss Mechanics\\n- **Miasma Attack**: The boss releases a toxic miasma cloud every 10 seconds that poisons nearby players. Can be countered with Cure potions or Fire Resistance.\\n- **Devastating Bite**: The boss lunges at nearby opponents, dealing 20 damage, healing itself for 25% of damage dealt, and gaining Resistance for 100 ticks.\\n- **High Health Pool**: Boss has 250 health and deals 15 base damage with 5 armor.\\n\\n### Summoning Recipe\\nCraft a **Summoning Catalyst** using:\\n```\\nB H B\\nH W H\\nB H B\\n```\\nWhere:\\n- B = Bone\\n- H = Wither Skeleton Head\\n- W = Wither Star (center)\\n\\nPlace the Summoning Catalyst on the ground to spawn the Undead Dragon Boss.\\n\\n### Dragon Claw Weapon\\nDefeating the boss drops **3x Dragon Claw** weapons with these features:\\n- **Damage**: 8 + Diamond tier base damage (10 damage total)\\n- **Durability**: 512 uses\\n- **Special Ability - Lunge**: Right-click (4 second cooldown) to perform a lunge attack that:\\n  - Launches the player forward in the direction they're looking\\n  - Deals 12 damage to entities hit\\n  - Knocks back enemies\\n  - Grants the player Resistance I for 100 ticks after hitting an enemy\\n  - Creates a dramatic sound effect\\n\\n## Installation\\n\\n1. Install Minecraft Forge 1.20.1 (version 47.3.0 or later)\\n2. Download the mod JAR file\\n3. Place it in your `mods` folder\\n4. Launch Minecraft with the Forge profile\\n\\n## Building from Source\\n\\n1. Clone the repository\\n2. Run `./gradlew build` (or `gradlew.bat build` on Windows)\\n3. The compiled JAR will be in `build/libs/`\\n4. Copy to your mods folder\\n\\n## Development\\n\\nThis mod is built with:\\n- Minecraft Forge 1.20.1\\n- Java 17\\n- Gradle build system\\n\\n## License\\n\\nMIT License - Feel free to use and modify as needed.\\n\\n## Countering Miasma\\n\\nThe miasma poison effect can be countered by:\\n1. Drinking a **Cure Potion** (if available)\\n2. Having **Fire Resistance** active\\n3. Staying away from the boss during miasma attacks\\n\\n## Tips for Boss Fight\\n\\n- The boss has a 200-tick cooldown between miasma attacks\\n- The bite attack only occurs when you're within 6 blocks\\n- Keep your distance to avoid the bite attack\\n- Use healing potions to sustain during the fight\\n- The boss only spawns one at a time - coordinate with other players if needed\\n- After defeat, collect the dragon claws to obtain powerful lunge weapons\\n\"}]}",

massive undead dragon boss with unique mechanics and powerful weapon drops.\\n\\n## Features\\n\\n### Boss Mechanics\\n- **Miasma Attack**: The boss releases a toxic miasma cloud every 10 seconds that poisons nearby players. Can be countered with Cure potions or Fire Resistance.\\n- **Devastating Bite**: The boss lunges at nearby opponents, dealing 20 damage, healing itself for 25% of damage dealt, and gaining Resistance for 100 ticks.\\n- **High Health Pool**: Boss has 250 health and deals 15 base damage with 5 armor.\\n\\n### Summoning Recipe\\nCraft a **Summoning Catalyst** using:\\n```\\nB H B\\nH W H\\nB H B\\n```\\nWhere:\\n- B = Bone\\n- H = Wither Skeleton Head\\n- W = Wither Star (center)\\n\\nPlace the Summoning Catalyst on the ground to spawn the Undead Dragon Boss.\\n\\n### Dragon Claw Weapon\\nDefeating the boss drops **3x Dragon Claw** weapons with these features:\\n- **Damage**: 8 + Diamond tier base damage (10 damage total)\\n- **Durability**: 512 uses\\n- **Special Ability - Lunge**: Right-click (4 second cooldown) to perform a lunge attack that:\\n  - Launches the player forward in the direction they're looking\\n  - Deals 12 damage to entities hit\\n  - Knocks back enemies\\n  - Grants the player Resistance I for 100 ticks after hitting an enemy\\n  - Creates a dramatic sound effect\\n\\n## Installation\\n\\n1. Install Minecraft Forge 1.20.1 (version 47.3.0 or later)\\n2. Download the mod JAR file\\n3. Place it in your `mods` folder\\n4. Launch Minecraft with the Forge profile\\n\\n## Building from Source\\n\\n1. Clone the repository\\n2. Run `./gradlew build` (or `gradlew.bat build` on Windows)\\n3. The compiled JAR will be in `build/libs/`\\n4. Copy to your mods folder\\n\\n## Development\\n\\nThis mod is built with:\\n- Minecraft Forge 1.20.1\\n- Java 17\\n- Gradle build system\\n\\n## License\\n\\nMIT License - Feel free to use and modify as needed.\\n\\n## Countering Miasma\\n\\nThe miasma poison effect can be countered by:\\n1. Drinking a **Cure Potion** (if available)\\n2. Having **Fire Resistance** active\\n3. Staying away from the boss during miasma attacks\\n\\n## Tips for Boss Fight\\n\\n- The boss has a 200-tick cooldown between miasma attacks\\n- The bite attack only occurs when you're within 6 blocks\\n- Keep your distance to avoid the bite attack\\n- Use healing potions to sustain during the fight\\n- The boss only spawns one at a time - coordinate with other players if needed\\n- After defeat, collect the dragon claws to obtain powerful lunge weapons\\n\"}]}",

Forge mod for version 1.20.1 that adds a massive undead dragon boss with unique mechanics, powerful weapon drops, a cure potion, and a dedicated Nether arena.\\n\\n## Features\\n\\n### Boss Mechanics\\n- **Miasma Attack**: The boss releases a toxic miasma cloud every 10 seconds that poisons nearby players. Can be countered with Cure potions.\\n- **Devastating Bite**: The boss lunges at nearby opponents, dealing 20 damage, healing itself for 25% of damage dealt, and gaining Resistance for 100 ticks.\\n- **High Health Pool**: Boss has 250 health and deals 15 base damage with 5 armor.\\n- **Boss Arena**: Automatic Nether arena generation with blackstone walls and nether brick flooring.\\n\\n### Summoning the Boss\\n1. Craft a **Summoning Catalyst** using:\\n   ```\\n   B H B\\n   H W H\\n   B H B\\n   ```\\n   Where:\\n   - B = Bone\\n   - H = Wither Skeleton Head\\n   - W = Wither Star (center)\\n\\n2. Travel to the **Nether** dimension\\n3. Use the Summoning Catalyst (right-click) to:\\n   - Automatically generate a massive arena with walls and pillars\\n   - Summon the Undead Dragon Boss at the center\\n\\n### Cure Potion\\nCounters the boss's miasma poison effect.\\n\\n**Cure Potion Recipe:**\\n```\\n G\\nGAG\\n G\\n```\\nWhere:\\n- G = Glowstone Dust\\n- A = Nether Wart\\n\\nCrafts 2 potions per recipe. Right-click (like any potion) to:\\n- Remove all poison effects\\n- Play a success sound\\n\\n### Dragon Claw Weapon\\nDefeating the boss drops **3x Dragon Claw** weapons with these features:\\n- **Damage**: 8 + Diamond tier base damage (10 damage total)\\n- **Durability**: 512 uses\\n- **Special Ability - Lunge**: Right-click (4 second cooldown) to perform a lunge attack that:\\n  - Launches the player forward in the direction they're looking\\n  - Deals 12 damage to entities hit\\n  - Knocks back enemies\\n  - Grants the player Resistance I for 100 ticks after hitting an enemy\\n  - Creates a dramatic dragon breath sound effect\\n\\n## Installation\\n\\n1. Install Minecraft Forge 1.20.1 (version 47.3.0 or later)\\n2. Download the mod JAR file\\n3. Place it in your `mods` folder\\n4. Launch Minecraft with the Forge profile\\n\\n## Building from Source\\n\\n1. Clone the repository\\n2. Run `./gradlew build` (or `gradlew.bat build` on Windows)\\n3. The compiled JAR will be in `build/libs/`\\n4. Copy to your mods folder\\n\\n## Boss Fight Strategy\\n\\n### Preparation\\n- Craft multiple Cure Potions to counter miasma\\n- Bring healing potions and food\\n- Wear full diamond or netherite armor\\n- Bring a strong sword or bow\\n\\n### During the Fight\\n- The boss has a 200-tick cooldown between miasma attacks (~10 seconds)\\n- Miasma poisoning can be cured with Cure Potions\\n- The bite attack only occurs when you're within 6 blocks\\n- Keep your distance and use ranged weapons when possible\\n- Use the arena pillars for cover\\n- Watch for the whispering sound effect before miasma attacks\\n\\n### After Victory\\n- Collect the 3 Dragon Claws dropped\\n- Use them to perform lunge attacks similar to the boss\\n- The lunge ability has a 4-second cooldown (80 ticks)\\n- Share claws with teammates for group combat advantage\\n\\n## Arena Structure\\n\\nThe Nether arena automatically generates with:\\n- **Circular design**: 60-block diameter arena\\n- **Blackstone walls**: 8 blocks high for protection\\n- **Nether brick floor**: Durable fighting surface\\n- **4 Corner pillars**: With soul fire on top for atmosphere and light\\n- **Safe spectator zone**: Outside the arena walls\\n\\n## Development\\n\\nThis mod is built with:\\n- Minecraft Forge 1.20.1\\n- Java 17\\n- Gradle build system\\n\\n## License\\n\\nMIT License - Boss Mod\\n\\nA Minecraft Forge mod for version 1.20.1 that adds a massive undead dragon boss with unique mechanics, powerful weapon drops, and a resurrection system.\\n\\n## ð Boss Mechanics\\n\\n### Boss Features\\n- **Miasma Attack**: The boss releases a toxic miasma cloud every 10 seconds that poisons nearby players.
